from recent rain. The water tastes faintly sweet and is always cool to the touch.
- Quirk: If thrown away, the hat reappears in the owner’s belongings within 1d6
hours.
- Weirding Twist: On rare occasions, when worn during sleep, the wearer
awakens with wet hair and shoes.
Snapping Spoon
A tarnished spoon that makes a snapping noise when it touches food.*
- Effect: The spoon emits a loud snap! when it touches anything edible, often
startling people at the dinner table.
- Quirk: It refuses to scoop liquids, passing through them without resistance.
- Weirding Twist: Some say the spoon occasionally swaps food between plates
without anyone noticing.
Glitching Candle
A simple beeswax candle that flickers erratically and occasionally emits strange
colors.*
- Effect: Once lit, the candle burns steadily for 1d8 hours, but every so often it
flickers with eerie green, blue, or purple light.
- Quirk: Shadows cast by the candle seem to move independently for a moment
when it flickers.
- Weirding Twist: If left burning in complete darkness, faint voices can be heard
whispering from the shadows, as if from another place or time.

# The Bestiary

Ryndor is a land full of majestic and powerful creatures, both wild and
domesticated. The people of Ryndor have a deep respect for the natural world and have
developed close relationships with many of the animals that inhabit their lands.
Travelers to Ryndor can expect to see many of these creatures in towns and cities,
where they are often used for transportation, labor, and protection. Visitors are
encouraged to treat these animals with respect and to learn more about the special
bonds that exist between them and the people of Ryndor.
Ryndor is home to a wide variety of magical creatures, both big and small. In the
meadows and forests, one might encounter the mischievous sprites, tiny beings with
butterfly-like wings who love to play pranks and can sometimes be convinced to offer
their aid. The fields and meadows are home to grigs, small, cricket-like creatures who
have a love for music and often play tiny instruments or sing in high-pitched voices.
For those traveling through the woods, they may come across pookas, small
shapeshifting creatures that can take the form of animals or objects and are known for
their love of mischief. In rivers, streams, and lakes, one might find nixies, water sprites
often depicted as beautiful maidens with gossamer wings, said to have the power to
control the flow of water.
In houses and other dwellings, brownies can be found. These small, helpful
creatures are known for their tidiness and their ability to complete household tasks
while their human occupants sleep. However, caution should be taken around imps,
small horned creatures with bat-like wings who are often associated with dark magic
and are known for causing chaos and confusion.
While the magical creatures of Ryndor can be wondrous and enchanting, there are
also those that are dangerous and potentially deadly. Travelers in Ryndor are advised to
exercise caution and avoid these dangerous creatures at all costs. It is also
recommended to seek the aid of a skilled hunter or ranger if traveling in areas where
these creatures are known to dwell.

## Domestic

Ryndor is a land full of majestic and powerful creatures, both wild and
domesticated. The people of Ryndor have a deep respect for the natural world and have
developed close relationships with many of the animals that inhabit their lands.
Travelers to Ryndor can expect to see many of these creatures in towns and cities,
where they are often used for transportation, labor, and protection. Visitors are
encouraged to treat these animals with respect and to learn more about the special
bonds that exist between them and the people of Ryndor.
Thornclaw Dragon
These small, green dragons have sharp claws and a venomous bite. They are often
used as guards or sentinels, and are valued for their ability to detect intruders with their
keen senses.

Dreamweaver Dragon
These ethereal dragons have iridescent scales that shimmer like opals. They can
create vivid illusions with their breath, and are often used as entertainers or in magical
performances.

Rustscale Dragon
These small, copper-colored dragons are often found in abandoned mines and
old ruins. They have a rusty breath weapon that can corrode metal and are valued by
some for their ability to help locate hidden treasure. These dragons are relatively
common and make great pets, so they might cost around 50-100 gold pieces each.

damage on a failed save, or half as much damage on a successful one.
Rusty Scales. The dragon has resistance to non-magical bludgeoning, piercing,
and slashing damage.
Emberglow Dragon
These small, bright red dragons are known for their fiery breath and their ability
to curl up in a ball of flames to protect themselves. They are a popular pet among
children. These dragons are relatively common and make great pets, so they might cost
around 50-100 gold pieces each.
Medium dragon, unaligned
Armor Class: 14 Hit Points: 22 (5d8) Speed: 30 ft., climb 20 ft., fly 60 ft.
STR 8 (-1) DEX 16 (+3) CON 10 (+0) INT 5 (-3) WIS 12 (+1) CHA 6 (-2)
Skills: Stealth +5 Senses: darkvision 60 ft., passive Perception 11 Languages:
understands Draconic but can't speak it
Fiery Breath (Recharge 5-6): The dragon exhales fire in a 15-foot cone. Each
creature in that area must make a DC 11 Dexterity saving throw, taking 14 (4d6) fire
damage on a failed save, or half as much damage on a successful one.
Flaming Ball: As an action, the dragon can curl up in a ball of flames. While in this
form, it has resistance to fire damage and can move through a space as narrow as 1 inch
wide without squeezing. The dragon can end this effect as a bonus action.
Sleipnir

cost: 5,000 - 10,000 gp
The Sleipnir resembles a massive eight-legged horse, but its form is anything
but natural. Towering nearly ten feet at the shoulder, it moves with an eerie elegance,
each of its eight legs placing itself in perfect synchronicity—as if time bends around its
gait. Its hooves never quite touch the ground; instead, they leave behind shimmering
ripples in space, like a stone skipped across still water.
Its coat is a shifting storm of color, rippling between coal black and deep violet, as
though clouds of the void swirl just beneath its skin. Strands of mane and tail float like
ink in water, trailing behind it in slow, sinuous ribbons that defy gravity and wind alike.
Its eyes—all four of them—glow softly with an inner light, silver and mournful,
never blinking. When it opens its mouth, it does not neigh; instead, it exhales a sound
like wind through hollow stone, or distant thunder whispered in reverse.
Sleipnir's supernatural speed and agility make it an excellent mount for those
who need to travel quickly. While riding Sleipnir, a character gains advantage on all
animal handling checks related to riding, and can travel an additional 10 miles per day
without suffering exhaustion.
Leighmore Oxen
cost: 500 - 1,000 gold pieces
Leighnmore oxen are incredibly strong and hardy, able to pull heavy loads and
work for long hours without tiring. While using a Leighmore ox as a beast of burden, a
character can carry an additional 500 pounds of weight without being encumbered, and
the ox can work for an additional 4 hours per day without suffering exhaustion.
Trollhound
cost: 1,000 - 2,000 gold pieces
Trollhounds are fiercely loyal and protective of their masters, making them
excellent guard animals. While a character has a trollhound as a pet or companion, they
have advantage on all perception checks made to detect enemies or intruders within 30
feet.
Dwarven Mule
cost: 750 - 1,500 gold pieces
Dwarven mules are incredibly strong and surefooted, able to navigate difficult
terrain and carry heavy loads without difficulty. While using a dwarven mule as a beast
of burden, a character gains advantage on all checks made to navigate rocky or
mountainous terrain, and can carry an additional 250 pounds of weight without being
encumbered.

## Cosmic

The Many Mouthed Mother
The Many-Mouthed Mother
The Many-Mouthed Mother is an immense and grotesque aberration, a fusion of

chaotic organic shapes with an ever-shifting form. Her body is a writhing mass of
warped flesh, covered in countless mouths of varying sizes, each constantly whispering,
laughing, or screaming. Eyes occasionally blink open across her undulating form, only
to disappear into the fleshy mass moments later. Her presence defies logic—her limbs
appear and vanish unpredictably, and parts of her form flicker between dimensions,
making it difficult to tell where she truly begins or ends. Her overwhelming size gives
the impression of a predator trapped between realities, eternally gnawing on both the
physical and metaphysical planes, desperate to consume anything that strays too close.
Her mouths are not just for feeding but also for channeling the maddening
influence of the Rift, filling the air with distorted whispers. This constant hum of sound
affects everything around her, inducing fear and madness in anyone nearby. Despite her
monstrous appearance, there is an unnerving beauty to her—her skin sometimes
glimmers like wet obsidian, and parts of her shimmer with ethereal hues that hint at the
strange energies she embodies.
Gargantuan Aberration (Patron of the Rift)
Alignment: Chaotic Evil
Armor Class: 19 (natural armor)
Hit Points: 395 (30d12 + 180)
Speed: 30 ft, swim 30 ft, burrow 15 ft
STR | DEX | CON | INT | WIS | CHA
28 (+9) | 12 (+1) | 22 (+6) | 19 (+4) | 16 (+3) | 24 (+7)
Saving Throws
Strength +15, Wisdom +9, Charisma +13
Skills
Deception +13, Insight +9, Perception +12
Damage Resistances
Cold, Psychic; Bludgeoning, Piercing, and Slashing from non-magical attacks
Damage Immunities
Poison, Acid
Condition Immunities
Charmed, Frightened, Exhaustion, Poisoned
Senses
Darkvision 120 ft., Truesight 60 ft., Passive Perception 22
Languages
Deep Speech, Telepathy 120 ft.
Traits

Many-Mouthed Aura. Creatures within 30 feet of the Many-Mouthed Mother

hear maddening whispers. At the start of their turn, they must succeed on a DC 18
Wisdom saving throw or take 3d8 psychic damage and be afflicted with short-term
madness for 1 minute (save ends at the end of each of their turns).
Riftborn Physiology. The Mother exists between dimensions. As a reaction, she
can shift out of sync with reality, granting herself resistance to all damage until the
start of her next turn.
Devourer’s Maw. The Mother can consume matter—both physical and magical.
When she reduces a creature to 0 hit points, she heals 30 hit points and gains advantage
on all saving throws until the end of her next turn.
Actions
Multiattack. The Many-Mouthed Mother makes three Bite attacks.
Bite. Melee Weapon Attack: +15 to hit, reach 10 ft., one target.
Hit: 28 (4d8 + 9) slashing damage, and the target must succeed on a DC 19
Strength saving throw or be grappled. While grappled, the target takes 10 (3d6) psychic
damage at the start of its turn.
Consume Magic (Recharge 5-6). The Mother devours a magical effect or spell. As
a reaction to being the target of a spell, she can end the spell and heal 1d8 hit points per
spell level. Creatures concentrating on the spell must make a DC 18 Intelligence saving
throw or take 4d10 psychic damage.
Mouths of Madness (1/Day). The Mother summons 1d4+2 mouths in unoccupied
spaces within 60 feet. These mouths act on her initiative, biting with a +9 to hit and
dealing 3d6 psychic damage. They last for 1 minute or until destroyed (AC 16, 30 HP
each).
Legendary Actions (3/Turn)
Swallow Reality. The Mother targets one creature within 30 feet, forcing it to
make a DC 18 Wisdom saving throw. On a failure, the creature’s soul is pulled halfway
into the Rift, rendering it incapacitated until the start of its next turn.
Shift Presence. The Mother teleports up to 40 feet to an unoccupied space she can
see.
Echoing Whispers. The Many-Mouthed Mother forces all creatures within 60
feet to make a DC 18 Wisdom saving throw. On a failure, they are frightened until the
end of their next turn.
The Many-Mouthed Mother represents the constant hunger of the Rift,
consuming minds, bodies, and souls alike. Her warlocks wield power at the cost of
sanity, drawing from her insatiable need to devour and grow.

## Wild

Hrimfaxi
The Hrimfaxi is a magnificent creature with a snow-white coat that shimmers
like diamonds in the sunlight. Its horn is a translucent crystal that glows with an icy
blue light, and its eyes are a piercing sapphire blue that seem to see right through you.
The Hrimfaxi's mane and tail are long and flowing, resembling streams of silver silk
that cascade down its back and legs. It stands tall and proud, with a regal bearing that
commands respect and admiration. As it moves, it leaves behind a trail of sparkling
snowflakes that seem to dance and twirl in the air. The Hrimfaxi is a rare and magical
sight, a symbol of the raw power and beauty of nature.
These creatures have a valuable horn that is sought after for its magical
properties. The Crystal Scholars have established strict regulations on the hunting and
capture of these animals, requiring permits and extensive documentation for any legal
capture. Additionally, they have established protected areas where Hrimfaxi can roam
freely and safely, and any unauthorized hunting or poaching is met with severe legal
consequences. The Scholars also work closely with local rangers and animal
conservationists to monitor the population and ensure that their numbers are
sustainable.
The horn of the Hrimfaxi is highly valued for its potent magical properties. When
ground into a fine powder and ingested, it is said to have powerful healing properties,
capable of curing even the most deadly of ailments. Additionally, it is believed that the
horn can enhance one's magical abilities, making it a sought-after ingredient for
potions and spells. Due to these properties, the horn is highly prized in the black
market, with poachers willing to risk the ire of the Crystal Scholars to obtain it.
Hrimfaxi

Harunvarp
The Harunvarp is a ferocious creature that dwells in the volcanic regions of
Ryndor. It has a bulky body covered in tough, dark-red scales, with large, muscular legs
that end in clawed feet. Its head is wide and flat, with two small, glowing eyes and a pair
of long, curved horns. From its mouth, the Harunvarp can shoot globs of molten lava at
its enemies, causing severe burns.
Despite its fearsome reputation, some brave adventurers have attempted to
domesticate Harunvarps, with varying degrees of success. Those who have managed to
befriend these creatures find them to be fiercely loyal and incredibly useful, particularly
in combat situations where their fiery abilities can turn the tide of battle.
Encountering a Harunvarp in the wild is not for the faint of heart, as these
creatures are notoriously territorial and will attack without hesitation if they feel
threatened. However, for those who are willing to take the risk, the rewards can be
great, as the scales, horns, and other parts of the Harunvarp are highly prized by
craftsmen and alchemists throughout Ryndor.
Hraunvarp

Galdrafell Vorpal
The Galdrafell Vorpals are a strange and chaotic creature that hails from the deep
oceans of Ryndor. They are unlike any other creature in the land, and their appearance
is both mesmerizing and terrifying.
The Vorpals are a large, gelatinous creature that pulsates with bioluminescent
light. They move through the water with incredible speed, leaving a trail of glowing
particles in their wake. Their body is adorned with long, thin tentacles that are covered
in sharp spines, and their large, gaping maw is filled with razor-sharp teeth.
The Galdrafell Vorpals are known for their incredibly loud and piercing screams,

which can shatter glass and disorient anyone within earshot. Their screams are often
used to stun and immobilize prey, allowing them to move in for the kill. They are also
able to emit a cloud of blinding ink, which they use to evade predators and confuse their
prey.
Despite their chaotic nature, the Galdrafell Vorpals are a delicacy in Ryndor, and
many fishermen brave the treacherous depths to catch them. Their flesh is said to be
sweet and tender, with a texture similar to that of squid. However, those who seek to
catch them must be careful, as the Vorpals are known to swarm and attack in large
numbers when threatened, and their screams can cause permanent hearing damage to
those who are not prepared.

# Choose Your Fate

In a world as vast and diverse as Ryndor, every face tells a story, and every soul
carries the essence of something greater. This chapter explores the many origins, paths,
and choices available to players, offering them the tools to shape characters as unique
as the world they inhabit. Whether molded by ancient bloodlines, empowered by the
mystical resonance of the astral plane, or drawn to fulfill a calling from within, the
people of Ryndor are as varied as the lands they tread.
Here, you will find new player options, including unique races, each carrying the
heritage of Ryndor’s turbulent history, and classes influenced by the balance between
magic, faith, and technology. These options allow players to embody characters with
deep connections to the world—whether they are a Sev’rinn attuned to elemental
forces, a Cervar druid communing with the natural realm, or a human adventurer
carving their destiny in the shifting tides of power.
This chapter offers a glimpse into the inner souls of these beings, exploring how
race, class, and essence intertwine. These options go beyond the surface—every culture,
tradition, and vocation reflects a belief, a struggle, or a dream rooted in the core of
Ryndor’s shifting balance. Some beings may draw power from the magic that saturates
the land, others from the divine, while some find strength in sheer will, cleverness, or
martial prowess.
In this chapter, you will encounter:
- New Races: Ancient and modern beings, each with a unique place in the world’s
evolving history.
- Expanded Backgrounds: Tailored to reflect the influence of faith, magic,
technology, and the Weirding upon the people of Ryndor.
- New Class Options: Paths from every walk of life, and every adventurous road,
that match the might land of Ryndor and its powerful influences
Each choice in this chapter is an invitation to immerse yourself in the souls and
identities that define the world of Ryndor. Will your character be shaped by the ancient
traditions of their ancestors or the mysteries born from the Rift to Nebernoria? Will they
bend to fate or defy it? In this land where every soul carries a spark, your choices matter
—not just to you, but to the story of the world itself.

## On Equal Footing

Races
The races of Ryndor are as varied and special as the land itself. In addition to the
races in the Player's Handbook, you can also choose from five new races.
Drakarim. In Ryndor, Drakarim are a rare and enigmatic race, known for their
strength, resilience, and deep connection to dragonkind.
Leporin. In Ryndor, Leoporin are a race of rabbit-like humanoids known for their
speed and agility. They are skilled hunters and gatherers, and often live in small, tightknit communities in the forest.
Aviari. Aviari in Ryndor are a rare sight, known for their aerial prowess and their

deep connection to the sky. They have a bird-like appearance with wings on their back,
talons on their feet, and beaks for their mouths.
Cervar. In Ryndor, Cervar are tall, slender, and graceful humanoids with deerlike features. They are are wise and gentle race, with a deep connection to the natural
world.
Nebernorian. Hailing from behind the rift, Nebernorians are a mysterious and
otherwordly race. Humanoid in appearance, they have elongated limbs and large
kaleidescope eyes.
Other Races
Gnomes
Gnomes in Ryndor are curious inventors and master tinkerers, known for their
boundless creativity. They thrive in academic and experimental fields, playing an
important role in blending magic with technology. Gnome communities often dwell in
hidden enclaves, working tirelessly on complex machinery or arcane research. Though
small in stature, gnomes wield impressive influence in the fields of artifice and
innovation, with many collaborating closely with the Crystal Scholars.
Gnome Names: Poppy, Fizzle, Tink, Bramble, and Wizzlewick. Surnames are
usually whimsical combinations of objects, such as Gearspindle or Clockwhistle.
Halflings
Halflings are community-oriented and practical, valuing friendship, home, and
tradition. They typically live in small rural villages, where they foster close-knit
communities that emphasize hard work and contentment. Despite their unassuming
nature, halflings are known for their cleverness and tenacity, and many have thrived as
merchants, explorers, or diplomats. They are particularly sought after as guides
through Ryndor’s complex political landscape, thanks to their keen perception and
adaptability.
Halfling Names: Milo, Rosie, Pippin, Ivy, and Thistle. Their surnames often
reflect nature or lifestyle, such as Greenhill or Goodbarrel.
Half-Elves
Half-elves walk the line between two worlds—carrying the grace and magical
aptitude of elves, but with the pragmatism and ambition of humans. They are often
mediators or diplomats, skilled at navigating cultural divides. Half-elves tend to feel
like outsiders, belonging to neither race entirely, and many find their place in
cosmopolitan cities like Eveltoft, where their dual heritage is an asset. They often
pursue roles as bards, scholars, or envoys, excelling at social interaction and problemsolving.
Half-Elf Names: A mix of human and elven names, such as Eryndor Windwalker
or Livia Brightwood.
Half-Orcs
Half-orcs in Ryndor embody strength, resilience, and determination. Descended
from orcish and human unions, they often struggle with prejudice but thrive in fields

where their tenacity and endurance shine—such as military or mercenary work. Many
half-orcs embrace the warrior’s path, but some pursue academic or spiritual roles,
eager to carve out new identities beyond their origins. Half-orcs are often found in
frontier regions, where their physical prowess and tactical skills are valued.
Half-Orc Names: Grak, Lura, Thokk, Morg, and Drugar. Their surnames often
reflect honorific titles or battle achievements, such as Ironfist or Bloodaxe.
Tieflings
Tieflings are individuals with infernal heritage, marked by horns, tails, and
glowing eyes, and often regarded with fear and suspicion. Despite their dark
reputation, many tieflings work to defy expectations, becoming respected figures in
magic, politics, or espionage. They tend to be independent and secretive, driven to
overcome prejudice and forge their own paths. Tieflings excel at deception, diplomacy,
and magic, often walking a fine line between temptation and virtue.
Tiefling Names: Zareth, Lilith, Voren, and Nyx. They may choose infernal names
or adopt aliases that reflect their ambitions, such as Shade or Fateborn.
Aviari
Aviari
Aviari in Ryndor are a rare sight, known for their aerial prowess and their deep
connection to the sky. They have a bird-like appearance with wings on their back, talons
on their feet, and beaks for their mouths. The Aviari are commonly seen as scouts,
patrolling the skies to keep an eye on the lands below. Their sharp vision and agility
make them excellent hunters, and they are respected for their role as the eyes of their
community.
Aviari are typically a solitary people, with only small, close-knit communities in
mountainous areas or remote cliffs. They are known for their complex vocalizations,
which allow them to communicate intricate messages over great distances. Despite
their independent nature, Aviari are known to form alliances with other races,
particularly those who share their love of the sky and adventure.
In Ryndor, Aviari have played a vital role in the defense of the region. During the
War of Benard Peak, a group of Aviari scouts provided vital intelligence to the allied
forces, which helped them plan their successful assault on the enemy stronghold. Their
contribution to the war effort was acknowledged by the leaders of the allied forces, who
granted them a place of honor in the victory celebration.
Aviari Lore
Long ago, the Aviari were believed to have descended from an ancient avian
species that possessed the ability to soar through the skies. Through generations of
adaptation and evolution, they developed a humanoid form with avian traits, allowing
them to navigate the skies with great agility and grace. It is said that the blessings of the
sky gods were bestowed upon them, bestowing the gift of flight and a deep connection
to the heavens.
As the Aviari evolved, their wings became stronger, their feathers more vibrant,

and their beaks sharper. They developed keen eyesight, capable of spotting prey from
great distances and discerning even the slightest movements in the air. Their talons
grew stronger, allowing them to grasp and manipulate objects with dexterity. Over
time, their bodies adapted to handle the demands of flight, becoming lighter and more
streamlined.
The Aviari developed a strong sense of community and reverence for the sky,
forming small, isolated settlements in high mountains or remote cliffs. They embraced
a nomadic lifestyle, exploring the vast skies and seeking new horizons. Their culture
became deeply intertwined with their aerial abilities, as they honed their skills as
scouts, messengers, and hunters. The Aviari's connection to the sky is not just physical
but spiritual as well, with their rituals and ceremonies centered around celestial events
and the shifting of the winds.
The Feather of Zephyr
Long ago, when the Aviari were still a young race finding their place in the world,
a significant event occurred that shaped their history.
It was during the Age of Ascendance that an ancient artifact known as the Feather
of Zephyr was discovered by an Aviari named Aeris Windrider. The Feather of Zephyr
was believed to be a gift from the gods, granting the possessor the ability to harness the
power of the winds themselves.
Aeris Windrider, a visionary and charismatic leader, became a figure of great
influence among the Aviari. With the Feather of Zephyr in his possession, he united the
scattered Aviari tribes and guided them towards a prosperous future. Under his
leadership, the Aviari developed advanced aerial combat techniques, honing their skills
as warriors and protectors of the sky. The legend of Aeris Windrider and the Feather of
Zephyr spread far and wide, cementing their place in Aviari folklore and history.
During this time, a powerful deity known as Aerasyl, the Skyward Sovereign,
emerged as a patron of the Aviari. Aerasyl bestowed her blessings upon the Aviari
people, enhancing their aerial abilities and granting them the gift of avian
communication. The Aviari revered Aerasyl as their protector and guide, building
temples and shrines dedicated to her throughout their settlements. The presence of
Aerasyl in their lives further solidified the Aviari's connection to the sky and their role
as guardians of the celestial realm.
The combination of the discovery of the Feather of Zephyr, the leadership of Aeris
Windrider, and the divine favor of Aerasyl propelled the Aviari into an era of prosperity
and strength. They became renowned throughout Ryndor for their aerial prowess and
their unwavering dedication to the sky. To this day, the Aviari cherish their history,
passing down tales of the Feather of Zephyr, the leadership of Aeris Windrider, and the
enduring influence of Aerasyl from one generation to the next.
Free Spirits
The Aviari possess a combination of traits that are influenced by their bird-like
nature and their connection to the sky. They are often characterized as free-spirited,
independent, and fiercely protective of their freedom. With an innate desire for

exploration and adventure, the Aviari are natural wanderers, always seeking new
horizons and uncharted territories.
Their close bond with the sky instills them with a sense of curiosity and wonder,
as they possess a deep appreciation for the natural world and its beauty. Aviari are
known to be perceptive, observant, and quick thinkers, honing their sharp senses to
navigate the skies and spot even the slightest details from great heights.
While they value their independence, the Aviari also understand the importance
of cooperation and unity. They form strong bonds within their small, close-knit
communities, fostering trust and loyalty among their kin. Aviari possess a deep
reverence for their ancestry and traditions, passing down stories and wisdom through
generations.
Their avian nature also influences their behavior, as they exhibit traits such as
adaptability, gracefulness, and a natural inclination for problem-solving. They are
skilled communicators, using a complex combination of vocalizations and body
language to convey messages and emotions.
Overall, the Aviari are a proud and noble race, embodying the spirit of the sky and
the freedom it represents. They value honor, loyalty, and the pursuit of knowledge,
making them valuable allies and respected members of the diverse races of Ryndor.
Mighty Wings
The Aviari possess a distinct avian appearance, with features that reflect their
close affinity with the sky. Standing at an average height of 5 to 6 feet, their bodies are
lean and agile, built for graceful flight. Their wingspan is generally proportional to their
height, spanning between 8 to 10 feet, allowing them to soar effortlessly through the air
currents.
Feathers cover the Aviari's body, ranging in colors and patterns that mimic the
diversity of birds in the natural world. The hues can vary from vibrant blues, greens,
and yellows, to earthy tones such as browns and grays, blending with their
surroundings. These plumage variations often represent the Aviari's lineage and
regional affiliations.
Their hands are equipped with sharp talons, which provide them with a firm grip
and aid in tasks such as hunting and climbing. Aviari have long, slender legs ending in
taloned feet, adapted for perching and agile movements. Their heads are adorned with a
distinct beak, used for various purposes, including eating, communication, and
preening their feathers.
In terms of lifespan, Aviari age at a similar rate to humans, reaching maturity in
their late teens and living up to around 70 years. They maintain their physical vitality
throughout their prime years, and even in old age, their aerial prowess remains
formidable. The weight of an Aviari can range from around 100 to 150 pounds, with
slight variations depending on individual build and plumage density.
Free Spirits
The Aviari possess a combination of traits that are influenced by their bird-like
nature and their connection to the sky. They are often characterized as free-spirited,

independent, and fiercely protective of their freedom. With an innate desire for
exploration and adventure, the Aviari are natural wanderers, always seeking new
horizons and uncharted territories.
Their close bond with the sky instills them with a sense of curiosity and wonder,
as they possess a deep appreciation for the natural world and its beauty. Aviari are
known to be perceptive, observant, and quick thinkers, honing their sharp senses to
navigate the skies and spot even the slightest details from great heights.
While they value their independence, the Aviari also understand the importance
of cooperation and unity. They form strong bonds within their small, close-knit
communities, fostering trust and loyalty among their kin. Aviari possess a deep
reverence for their ancestry and traditions, passing down stories and wisdom through
generations.
Their avian nature also influences their behavior, as they exhibit traits such as
adaptability, gracefulness, and a natural inclination for problem-solving. They are
skilled communicators, using a complex combination of vocalizations and body
language to convey messages and emotions.
Overall, the Aviari are a proud and noble race, embodying the spirit of the sky and
the freedom it represents. They value honor, loyalty, and the pursuit of knowledge,
making them valuable allies and respected members of the diverse races of Ryndor.
Friends to All
The Aviari have diverse relationships with the races of Ryndor. Humans are
fascinated by their aerial abilities, while elves share a mutual respect for nature. They
form harmonious partnerships with Leoporin, appreciating each other's agility, and
work as scouts for the Drakarim despite their contrasting natures. The Aviari and Cervar
have a mutually beneficial relationship, combining their skills for successful hunts.
Overall, the Aviari are valued allies and respected members of the diverse races, finding
common ground and cooperation with those who appreciate their unique abilities and
perspectives.
Humans: The Aviari and humans have a mixed relationship. Some humans are
fascinated by the Aviari's ability to soar through the sky and view them with awe and
admiration. Others may view them as strange or distant due to their bird-like features.
However, there have been instances of cooperation between Aviari scouts and human
adventurers, working together to explore new frontiers or gather valuable information.
Elves: The Aviari and elves share a mutual respect and understanding of the
natural world. Both races possess a deep connection to nature and appreciate its beauty.
They often find common ground in their shared love for the wilderness and can form
alliances to protect and preserve the natural realms.
Leoporin: The Aviari and Leoporin share a harmonious relationship, as both races
appreciate freedom and independence. They admire each other's agility and
adaptability, often working together as scouts and messengers. The Aviari's ability to
navigate the skies complements the Leoporin's expertise in terrestrial environments,
making them effective partners in various endeavors.
Drakarim: The Aviari and Drakarim have a distant relationship due to their

contrasting natures. The Aviari's light-hearted and free-spirited nature can clash with
the more serious and reserved demeanor of the Drakarim. However, they share a mutual
respect for each other's strength and determination. It is not uncommon for the Aviari
to act as aerial scouts for the Drakarim, providing valuable information from the skies.
Cervar: The Aviari and Cervar often have a mutually beneficial relationship. The
Cervar, being skilled hunters and trackers, appreciate the Aviari's keen eyesight and
ability to spot prey from above. In return, the Aviari value the Cervar's ability to
navigate the forests and provide ground-based support during expeditions. Together,
they form formidable hunting parties and work in tandem to secure resources.
Home in the Clouds
The ancestral lands of the Aviari are a breathtaking expanse of rugged mountains,
deep valleys, and expansive sky. Nestled amidst these natural wonders are their sacred
sites and cherished havens.
One such place is Aetherwing Cliff, a towering precipice where Aviari gather for
important rituals and communal gatherings. The Great Perch, a majestic stone
formation jutting out from a mountaintop, serves as a revered meeting place and a
lookout point for vigilant sentinels.
The Azure Glades, a verdant valley dotted with shimmering pools and cascading
waterfalls, is a serene haven where Aviari retreat for reflection and spiritual connection
with nature. Highwind Canyon, a windswept gorge with narrow ledges and treacherous
currents, is both a testing ground for Aviari warriors and a training site for mastering
aerial maneuvers.
The Aviari capital, Skyrise Citadel, stands proudly atop the highest peak in the
ancestral lands. This magnificent city of intricate towers and soaring spires is a hub of
Aviari culture, housing the Council of Feathers and serving as a center for learning,
trade, and governance.
Throughout these lands, Aviari find solace, purpose, and a deep connection to the
sky and the natural world that surrounds them. The Aviari's ancestral lands embody the
essence of freedom, adventure, and the boundless possibilities that come with soaring
through the heavens.
Sounds of the Sky
Auran, the language of the Aviari, is a melodious and ethereal tongue that reflects
their deep connection to the sky and the winds. It is characterized by its flowing
cadence, graceful intonations, and a rich variety of vocalizations that mimic the sounds
of nature and the songs of birds.
Auran incorporates a wide range of pitch and tonal inflections, with soaring highs
and gentle lows, evoking the ever-changing currents of the wind. The language is not
solely based on spoken words but also includes an intricate system of whistles, trills,
clicks, and soft murmurs, allowing the Aviari to convey complex meanings and
emotions with remarkable precision.
In written form, Auran utilizes elegant, flowing scripts inspired by the curves and
movements of avian wings. The written symbols often resemble feathers, with intricate

patterns and graceful arcs that represent the harmony and interconnectedness of the
Aviari with their natural surroundings.
Auran is not just a means of communication for the Aviari; it is a poetic
expression of their identity and a profound connection to the elemental forces of the
sky. The language is steeped in tradition and is integral to their culture, passed down
through generations as a treasured legacy. Through Auran, the Aviari express their
thoughts, share their stories, and preserve their history, perpetuating their bond with
the skies that have always been their home.
Aviari Phrases
"Feathers intertwined create unbreakable bonds."
Symbolizing the importance of strong relationships and the support of loved
ones.
"A soaring heart knows no boundaries."
Meaning that one's spirit and determination can overcome any obstacle.
"Brush of a feather is the touch of truth."
Signifying the importance of paying attention to subtle cues and trusting one's
instincts.
Wanderlust
The Aviari are driven to adventure by their insatiable wanderlust and thirst for
exploration. The vast open skies call to their souls, urging them to soar beyond their
familiar territories and discover new lands. They seek to expand their knowledge,
unravel the mysteries of the world, and experience the exhilaration of soaring to great
heights.
Curiosity fuels their desire to venture into uncharted realms, where they can
witness breathtaking vistas, encounter diverse cultures, and forge new alliances. The
Aviari are drawn to the thrill of the unknown, the excitement of encountering ancient
ruins or hidden treasures, and the chance to test their aerial prowess in daring feats.
Ranger: The Aviari's keen senses and affinity for nature make them excellent
rangers. They can scout the vast landscapes from above, utilizing their aerial advantage
to track targets, navigate treacherous terrains, and communicate with animals. Their
ability to swiftly strike from the skies with precise archery skills makes them formidable
hunters and protectors of the wild.
Rogue: The Aviari's agility, stealth, and exceptional vision make them adept
rogues. Their wings provide them with unmatched mobility, allowing them to swiftly
navigate urban environments and bypass obstacles. With their sharp senses, they excel
in scouting, gathering information, and performing precise aerial maneuvers to
outmaneuver foes.
Sorcerer: The Aviari's connection to the sky and their innate magical affinity
make them ideal sorcerers. They possess a deep well of raw arcane power, drawing
inspiration from the natural elements and the boundless energy of the heavens. They
can manipulate air currents, conjure storms, or channel their magic through their

wings, becoming a force to be reckoned with on the battlefield.
Bard: The melodious nature of the Aviari's vocalizations and their ability to
communicate over long distances make them natural bards. They weave enchanting
melodies that evoke emotions and inspire allies. Their songs, combined with their
graceful aerial performances, captivate audiences and have the power to sway hearts
and minds.
Monk: The Aviari's dexterity, grace, and mastery of their own bodies align well
with the monk class. They have honed their physical abilities through years of
disciplined training, incorporating their aerial prowess into their combat techniques.
Their swift strikes, evasive maneuvers, and ability to harness their inner energy make
them formidable warriors.
Aviari Traits
Ability Score Increase Your Dexterity score increases by 2, and your Wisdom
score increases by 1.
Age Aviari mature quickly, reaching adulthood around age 3, and can live up to 30
years.
Alignment Aviari tend towards chaotic alignments, but can vary widely based on
their individual experiences.
Size Aviari are about the same size as humans, ranging from 5 to 6 feet tall on
average. Your size is Medium.
Speed Your base walking speed is 30 feet. You also have a flying speed of 30 feet,
but you cannot fly if you are wearing medium or heavy armor, or if you are encumbered.
Languages You can speak, read, and write Common and Auran.
Flightless You cannot use your wings to fly until you reach 5th level, at which
point you gain the ability to fly for short periods of time. You must land at the end of
your turn if you are flying, unless you are able to hover.
Keen Sight You have proficiency in the Perception skill.
Mimicry You can mimic sounds you have heard, such as voices, animal sounds, or
environmental sounds. You must have heard the sound for at least 1 minute to mimic it
accurately.
Cervar
Cervar
Cervar are tall, slender, and graceful humanoids with deer-like features. They
have slender legs ending in cloven hooves, and their arms are more delicate than
humans', with long, nimble fingers. Cervar have long, slender necks and elegant heads
with deer-like features such as large, expressive eyes, and pointed ears. Their hair is
usually thick and wavy, and they tend to have a variety of natural colors, including
brown, blonde, white, and even silver.
Cervar are a wise and gentle race, with a deep connection to the natural world.
They have a natural talent for magic and often use their abilities to heal and protect the
forests and animals of Ryndor. Cervar have a strong affinity for the natural world, and
their society revolves around their connection to it. They are peaceful beings who seek

to live in harmony with nature and avoid conflict whenever possible.
The Cervar's unique physiology provides them with a few special abilities. They
have keen senses that allow them to detect things that are far away, and their hooves
make them fast runners and agile jumpers. Additionally, their natural magic abilities
allow them to cast spells that protect and heal themselves and their allies, making them
valuable allies in any adventuring party.
Cervar Lore
The Cervar's connection to magic plays a vital role in their evolution. Their
natural talent for magic is believed to have evolved as a response to the magical
energies present in their surroundings. Living in harmony with nature, the Cervar
developed a deep affinity for the natural world and its energies. Through generations of
exposure and practice, their innate magical abilities became refined, enabling them to
harness the powers of healing and protection. This affinity for magic is deeply ingrained
in their society and is passed down through their cultural practices and teachings.
As the Cervar embraced their magical heritage, they further honed their abilities
to serve as guardians of the forests and caretakers of the animals in their realm. They
developed a profound understanding of the delicate balance of nature, using their magic
to heal wounded creatures, protect the environment from harm, and commune with the
spirits of the forest.
While the Cervar evolved physically and magically, their wisdom and gentle
nature also played a significant role in shaping their society. Their inclination towards
peaceful coexistence and harmony with nature guided their interactions with other
races and communities. They became known as wise beings, sought after for their
counsel and healing abilities.
Wielders of the Light
he history of the Cervar is rich with tales of discovery, leadership, and triumph
over evil forces.
Over the centuries, they have faced various challenges, but their unwavering
connection to nature and their innate magic has guided them through tumultuous
times.
One significant event in Cervar history was the discovery of a powerful artifact
known as the Elysian Crystal. Legends foretold of its existence, and the Cervar, with
their deep understanding of magic, were drawn to seek out this extraordinary relic. It
was said to possess immense healing and protective properties, capable of restoring
balance and harmony to the land. After years of exploration and dedicated research, a
group of Cervar mages uncovered the ancient ruins that housed the Elysian Crystal.
The discovery of the Elysian Crystal had a profound impact on the Cervar society.
Recognizing its potential to amplify their magical abilities and aid in their quest to
safeguard the natural world, the Cervar formed a council of wise elders to oversee the
artifact's use. The crystal became a symbol of hope and unity among the Cervar,
reinforcing their commitment to their role as protectors and healers of the land.
During this time, a charismatic and influential Cervar leader emerged, known as

Elara Sunwhisper. Possessing remarkable magical abilities and a deep connection to the
natural world, Elara became a beacon of guidance and inspiration for her people. Under
her wise and compassionate leadership, the Cervar society flourished. Elara fostered an
era of enlightenment and sought to strengthen the bonds between the Cervar and other
races, promoting peace and cooperation.
However, the rise of an influential leader also attracted the attention of dark
forces seeking to exploit the Cervar's magical prowess and disrupt their harmonious
way of life. A malevolent sorcerer named Morvath the Corruptor, driven by power and
domination, sought to harness the energy of the Elysian Crystal for his nefarious
purposes. Morvath gathered an army of corrupted creatures and waged a war against
the Cervar and their allies.
The Cervar, with their deep connection to nature and their mastery of magic,
rallied to defend their homeland against Morvath's forces. Their swift footwork and
agile maneuvers allowed them to outmaneuver their enemies, while their healing and
protective spells proved invaluable in sustaining their allies in battle. With Elara at the
forefront, leading her people with wisdom and unwavering determination, the Cervar
resisted Morvath's advances.
The conflict between the Cervar and Morvath culminated in an epic showdown.
Elara, drawing upon the energies of the Elysian Crystal and channeling the collective
magic of her people, engaged Morvath in a fierce duel. With the aid of her fellow Cervar
and their combined magical prowess, Elara managed to defeat the sorcerer, sealing him
away in a pocket dimension, forever preventing him from causing harm to Ryndor.
The victory over Morvath the Corruptor marked a turning point in Cervar history.
It solidified their reputation as protectors of the natural world and cemented their
commitment to maintaining harmony and balance. The tale of Elara Sunwhisper and
the defeat of Morvath became a legend passed down through generations, inspiring
future Cervar leaders and reminding them of the strength that can be found in unity,
wisdom, and the power of their connection to nature.
From that point forward, the Cervar continued to thrive, using their magic to heal
the wounded, protect the forests, and promote harmony between races. Their history
serves as a testament to their resilience, wisdom, and unwavering dedication to the
principles that define their existence.
Simplicity and Harmony
The Cervar possess a distinct personality and nature that reflects their deep
connection to the natural world. They are known for their wisdom, gentleness, and
harmonious disposition, embodying qualities that align with their role as caretakers
and protectors of the forests and animals of Ryndor.
Their gentle and compassionate nature extends not only to the natural world but
also to their interactions with others. Cervar are typically peaceful beings who seek to
resolve conflicts through diplomacy and understanding. They value harmony and
cooperation, and strive to maintain amicable relationships with other races and
communities. They possess a deep empathy that allows them to intuitively understand
the emotions and needs of those around them.

In their day-to-day lives, the Cervar value simplicity and harmony. They find
solace in the tranquility of the forests and often engage in activities that strengthen
their bond with nature, such as communing with the spirits of the forest, practicing
meditation, or engaging in creative pursuits that celebrate the beauty of the natural
world. They have a deep appreciation for art, music, and storytelling, often using these
mediums to express their connection to nature and share their wisdom with others.
Peaceful Presence
The Cervar are an enchanting and graceful race, resembling tall, slender
humanoids with deer-like features. Their elegant physique is defined by long, slender
legs ending in cloven hooves, and delicate, nimble arms with 3 slender fingers. Cervar
bodies are covered in soft fur with various patterns and markings denoting their native
land.
Though subtle differences exist, both genders possess delicate features, with soft,
regal faces. The have large, expressive eyes, and flat black or pink noses. Both male and
female Cervar bear striking antlers, often adorned with flowers and symbols of their
home land. Elongated, pointed ears crown their heads, attuned to the whispers of the
forest. Their hair, thick and wavy, mirrors the hues of the natural world, enhancing
their ethereal beauty. With heights ranging from 6 to 7 feet, the Cervar exude elegance
and agility. Their lean physiques, toned with muscles, reflect their inherent athleticism.
The Cervar's captivating presence is not limited by age. With lifespans ranging
from 150 to 200 years, they retain their youthful appearance long into their later years.
Throughout their lives, the Cervar embody a profound connection to nature, their
physicality and wisdom intertwined, a testament to their role as caretakers and
guardians of harmony in the world.
Gentle Allies
The Cervar, with their gentle and harmonious nature, strive to maintain positive
relationships with the other races of Ryndor. Their deep connection to nature often
fosters a sense of understanding and empathy towards others, allowing them to find
common ground and build alliances based on shared values. Here is an overview of the
relationships between the Cervar and the various races of Ryndor:
Leoporin: The Cervar share a particularly close bond with the Leoporin, a feline
humanoid race. Both races possess a deep respect for the natural world and have a
strong affinity for the forest. The Cervar appreciate the Leoporin's agility and keen
senses, while the Leoporin admire the wisdom and magical abilities of the Cervar.
Together, they often collaborate to protect and preserve the delicate ecosystems of
Ryndor, working in harmony to ensure the well-being of the land.
Drakarim: The relationship between the Cervar and the Drakarim, a reptilian
humanoid race, is more complex. Initially, their differences in temperament and values
created tensions, as the Drakarim were seen as more aggressive and territorial
compared to the peaceful Cervar. However, over time, the Cervar's wisdom and ability
to find common ground helped bridge the gap. Through dialogue and understanding,
they have forged alliances to address threats that endanger the natural world,

recognizing the importance of cooperation in preserving the balance of Ryndor.
Aviari: The Aviari, a winged humanoid race, find kinship with the Cervar in their
shared affinity for the skies and the creatures that dwell above. The Cervar admire the
Aviari's graceful flight and their ability to navigate the aerial realms. The Aviari, in turn,
appreciate the Cervar's wisdom and their dedication to preserving the natural world.
Together, they work to protect the diverse ecosystems that exist both on the ground and
in the sky, fostering a strong partnership that spans the domains of earth and air.
Humans: The Cervar's interactions with Humans are marked by a mutual respect
for each other's strengths and capabilities. The Cervar appreciate the ingenuity and
adaptability of the Human race, while the Humans recognize the Cervar's deep
connection to nature and their healing and magical abilities. The Cervar often serve as
guides and mentors, sharing their wisdom and offering guidance on matters related to
the natural world. Human-Cervar collaborations frequently arise in endeavors to
protect the environment and promote ecological balance.
Elves: The relationship between the Cervar and the Elves is one of mutual
admiration and shared affinity. Both races have a deep reverence for nature and possess
a profound connection to the mystical energies of the world. The Cervar respect the
Elven craftsmanship and their innate magical talents, while the Elves appreciate the
Cervar's wisdom and their dedication to preserving the natural harmony. Together,
they collaborate in safeguarding ancient forests and mystical realms, united in their
efforts to maintain the balance of Ryndor.
Dwarves: The Cervar and Dwarves have differing perspectives and priorities, but
their relationship is built on mutual respect and understanding. The Dwarves' affinity
for craftsmanship and mining starkly contrasts with the Cervar's focus on the natural
world. However, the Cervar acknowledge the Dwarves' dedication and industriousness,
while the Dwarves value the Cervar's wisdom and their magical abilities. Although their
collaboration may be less frequent, they find common ground in protecting shared
environments and addressing threats that endanger the land.
Verdant Glades
The ancestral lands of the Cervar are known as the Verdant Glades, a vast and
breathtaking realm of pristine wilderness. Within this realm, specific places hold deep
significance to the Cervar. Solara's Grove is a sacred grove where the Cervar gather for
spiritual ceremonies and seek guidance from the spirits of the forest. Starlight Falls is a
captivating waterfall that shimmers like starlight under the moon, offering solace and
inspiration to the Cervar. The Whispering Woods, an ancient forest, is revered for its
mystical aura and serves as a sanctuary for rituals and communion with nature.
Serenity Lake, a tranquil body of water, holds mystical properties that enhance the
Cervar's connection to nature and their magical abilities. Lastly, Harmony Grove, with
its ancient trees, symbolizes the harmony between all living beings and serves as a place
of communal activities and celebrations.
These locations within the Verdant Glades embody the Cervar's deep reverence
for nature and their commitment to its preservation. They are more than physical
landscapes; they are spiritual sanctuaries where the Cervar find solace, seek wisdom,

and celebrate the interconnectedness of all living things. The Verdant Glades and its
sacred places reflect the Cervar's profound connection to the natural world and their
role as caretakers and guardians of the land they hold dear.
Enchanting Words
The language of the Cervar, known as Enchantian, is a melodic and expressive
form of communication that embodies their deep connection with nature and their
harmonious way of life. Enchantian is characterized by its musicality, with a rhythmic
flow that resembles a lyrical song. The language draws inspiration from the natural
world, with a vocabulary rich in terms describing plants, animals, and natural
phenomena. Enchantian allows the Cervar to express a wide range of emotions and
sentiments with precision and depth, using gentle and harmonious sounds that mirror
their peaceful nature. It also possesses a telepathic aspect, enabling the Cervar to
communicate directly through thoughts and emotions. Enchantian serves as a beautiful
means of fostering understanding, unity, and a profound connection with both their
fellow Cervar and the natural environment they cherish.
Cervar Phrases
"When the moon weeps, the forest listens."
This proverb signifies the attentiveness and empathy they have towards the
environment, understanding that even the smallest changes can have a profound
impact.
"Like the river's current, adapt with grace."
his saying encourages individuals to flow through life's obstacles with grace and
resilience, just as a river navigates its course amidst various terrains.
"The dance of light reveals hidden paths."
This saying encourages individuals to seek out the hidden truths and possibilities
that may be concealed within challenges and uncertainties, as they can lead to
unexpected and enlightening paths.
In All Things, Harmony
The religion of the Cervar centers around their deep reverence for nature and the
spiritual connection they share with the natural world.
They view nature as a manifestation of the divine and engage in rituals and
ceremonies that celebrate its sacredness. Through their beliefs, they recognize the
intricate interplay between the physical and spiritual realms, guided by the notion of a
divine life force that permeates all living things.
At the heart of their religious practices is the worship of nature itself. The Cervar
hold a profound respect for the elements of the natural world, honoring the changing
seasons, the cycles of life and death, and the overall harmony that exists within the
environment. They celebrate these aspects through rituals and ceremonies that
incorporate music, dance, and offerings to the spirits and deities associated with nature.
The Cervar also hold a strong belief in spirit guardians who watch over and

protect specific aspects of nature. These guardians serve as intermediaries between the
Cervar and the divine, offering guidance, wisdom, and protection. Additionally, the
Cervar hold their ancestors in high regard, believing in their continued presence and
influence in the spiritual realm. They honor their ancestors through ancestral rites and
rituals, seeking their guidance and drawing upon their wisdom.
Central to the Cervar's religious beliefs is the pursuit of balance and harmony.
They strive to live in harmony with nature, recognizing the importance of nurturing the
delicate balance within the natural world. By doing so, they align themselves with the
divine forces and contribute to the greater harmony of the universe.
Destiny Awaits
Driven by their connection to nature, desire for knowledge, compassion, personal
growth, and a sense of destiny, the Cervar may find themselves compelled to embark on
adventures. Whether it is protecting the natural world from threats, seeking wisdom
and enlightenment, assisting friends and allies, pursuing personal growth, or
answering a call of destiny, these motivations ignite their sense of adventure. Despite
their peaceful nature, the Cervar understand that stepping outside their comfort zone,
facing challenges, and exploring the unknown can lead to profound personal
development and contribute to the greater balance and harmony of their world.
Druid: The Druid class embodies the Cervar's affinity for nature and their ability
to harness its power. Druids have a strong connection to the natural world, can shapeshift into animal forms, and wield powerful nature-based spells. Their ability to
communicate with animals and manipulate the environment aligns perfectly with the
Cervar's deep understanding and respect for the natural world.
Ranger: The Ranger class shares a kinship with the Cervar's skills and focus.
Rangers are skilled trackers, archers, and wilderness experts. They excel in scouting,
surviving in the wild, and protecting nature from threats. The Ranger's spells and
abilities that enhance their combat prowess and tracking abilities resonate with the
Cervar's role as guardians of the natural world.
Cleric (Nature Domain): The Nature Domain within the Cleric class is a natural fit
for the Cervar. Clerics of the Nature Domain draw power from the forces of nature,
wielding spells that heal and protect. They have a deep connection to the divine aspect
of the natural world and can call upon the powers of nature to aid their allies and smite
their enemies.
Bard (College of Lore or College of Glamour): Bards possess a versatile skill set
and can weave magic through their performances. The College of Lore emphasizes
knowledge and versatility, allowing bards to draw upon the wisdom and stories of the
natural world. The College of Glamour, on the other hand, focuses on enchantment and
charm, reflecting the Cervar's graceful and alluring nature.
Monk (Way of the Four Elements): Monks who follow the Way of the Four
Elements can harness elemental powers, which aligns with the Cervar's affinity for
natural magic. By channeling their inner energy, they can unleash elemental attacks
and manipulate the environment. This class option allows the Cervar to blend martial

arts prowess with the natural forces that surround them.
Cervar Traits
The Cervar's magical healing ability, Healing Touch, draws upon their connection
to the natural world, allowing them to channel the life energy of the forests and
meadows to heal others. Their long lifespan and appreciation for balance and harmony
reflect their affinity for the natural world, and their ability to move swiftly through it is
reflected in their fast speed. With their Fey Ancestry and proficiency in the Nature skill,
Cervar are well-suited to navigating the wilderness and dealing with the fey creatures
that often inhabit it.
Ability Score Increase Your Wisdom score increases by 2 and your Constitution
score increases by 1.
Age Cervar mature at a rate similar to humans but live longer, up to 250 years.
Alignment Cervar tend to be neutral or good, valuing balance and harmony.
Size Cervar are medium-sized creatures, typically standing between 5 and 6 feet
tall and weighing between 150 and 200 pounds.
Speed Your base walking speed is 35 feet.
Languages You can speak, read, and write Common and Sylvan.
Healing Touch As an action, you can touch a creature and cause it to regain a
number of hit points equal to your level + your Wisdom modifier. You can use this
feature a number of times equal to your Wisdom modifier (minimum of once), and you
regain all expended uses of it after a long rest.
Fey Ancestry You have advantage on saving throws against being charmed, and
magic can't put you to sleep.
Nature's Blessing You have proficiency in the Nature skill.
Drakarim
Drakarim
In Ryndor, Drakarim are a rare and enigmatic race, known for their strength,
resilience, and deep connection to dragonkind. They are humanoid in form, with
reptilian features such as scales, tails, and sharp teeth. Their skin can range in color
from deep red to metallic gold, and their eyes are often slit-pupiled and glow with an
inner fire.
Drakarim have a long and storied history in Ryndor, with many legends and
myths surrounding their origins. Some say that they were created by the ancient
dragons as their loyal servants and guardians, while others believe that they are the
descendants of humans who made pacts with dragon deities.
Drakarim Lore
The ancestral origin of the Drakarim is steeped in ancient tales and the echoes of
forgotten times. According to the legends passed down through generations, the
Drakarim trace their lineage back to a time when the world was young and dragons
reigned supreme. It is said that the great dragons, in their wisdom and power, chose
certain humans to become their chosen kin, granting them the blood of the dragon and

transforming them into the first Drakarim.
The process of transformation was a sacred ritual performed by the dragons
themselves, involving a mystical bond between the chosen humans and their dragon
benefactors. Through this bond, the essence of the dragons infused their mortal kin,
altering their physical form and infusing them with the inherent traits and abilities of
dragonkind.
The Dragonheart Shard
In the annals of Drakarim history, the evolution of their race is marked by
significant events and the rise of influential figures who shaped their destiny. Ages ago,
during a tumultuous period of dragon-human coexistence, a profound discovery altered
the course of Drakarim evolution. It was the unearthing of an ancient artifact known as
the Dragonheart Shard—a crystalline fragment said to contain a portion of a mighty
dragon's essence. This artifact became a focal point for the Drakarim's connection to
their dragon kin.
The Dragonheart Shard resonated with the Drakarim, awakening latent dragonic
powers within them and deepening their bond with dragons. This discovery sparked a
transformative era, as Drakarim individuals began to exhibit heightened physical traits,
such as stronger scales and heightened senses. The artifact also bestowed a deeper
understanding of dragon magic, allowing the Drakarim to channel the elemental forces
associated with dragons.
Amidst this evolving landscape, one Drakarim leader emerged as a figure of
profound influence—Vaelthar the Dragonheart. Vaelthar was a charismatic warrior and
visionary, who rallied his people during a time of external threats and internal strife.
With the aid of the Dragonheart Shard, Vaelthar united various Drakarim clans under
his banner, forging a powerful alliance that extended beyond blood ties.
Under Vaelthar's guidance, the Drakarim rose to prominence as formidable
defenders and protectors. Vaelthar's legendary feats of valor and strategic brilliance
became the stuff of legend, inspiring generations of Drakarim warriors to embrace their
draconic heritage. His reign marked an era of relative stability and prosperity for the
Drakarim, fostering alliances with dragons and forging new traditions that celebrated
the harmony between their races.
The legacy of Vaelthar the Dragonheart endures as a symbol of the Drakarim's
resilience and their unyielding dedication to the cause of dragonkind. His story serves as
a reminder of the crucial role played by influential leaders in shaping the destiny of the
Drakarim race.
Stoic Countenance
The Drakarim people possess a distinct nature and personality that reflects their
deep connection to dragonkind. They are known for their inherent strength, resilience,
and an unwavering sense of honor and loyalty. The legacy of their draconic heritage is
evident in their physical features, such as their scales, tails, and sharp teeth, as well as
their vibrant, fiery eyes that reflect their inner power.
Driven by a strong sense of community and a deep reverence for their dragon

allies, the Drakarim exhibit a disciplined and disciplined mindset. They are a proud race,
valuing tradition and upholding ancient customs that emphasize honor, bravery, and
the preservation of their ancestral heritage. Drakarim individuals are often raised with a
profound respect for authority and hierarchy, recognizing the wisdom of their elders
and leaders.
Despite their imposing presence and warrior-like demeanor, Drakarim possess
an innate wisdom and a deep understanding of the delicate balance between power and
responsibility. They have a natural affinity for magic, particularly that which is tied to
dragons and the elemental forces. This affinity manifests in their ability to harness and
channel dragon magic, allowing them to wield fire, thunder, and other forces associated
with their draconic kin.
In social interactions, Drakarim exhibit a sense of stoicism and self-control,
rarely displaying overt emotions. They prioritize logic and reason, making them highly
pragmatic and adept problem solvers. However, their fierce loyalty and protective
instincts can drive them to great lengths to defend their kin, allies, and their cherished
dragon companions.
Imposing Presence
The Drakarim possess a distinctive and awe-inspiring physical appearance that
sets them apart from other humanoid races. They typically stand tall, ranging from 6 to
7 feet in height, with a strong and muscular build that reflects their natural prowess in
combat. Their reptilian features include scaly skin that varies in color from deep red to
metallic gold, giving them a striking and majestic presence.
In terms of weight, Drakarim tend to be heavier than other races due to their
muscular physique. On average, they weigh between 200 and 300 pounds, though the
weight can vary depending on the individual's size and physical conditioning.
The physical maturity of a Drakarim is comparable to that of humans, with an
average age range of up to 120 years, usually reaching maturity around 20-25. However,
some Drakarim who have formed powerful bonds with dragons or have attained great
knowledge and mastery of dragon magic can live well beyond a century.
Drakarim reproduction follows a method similar to that of other humanoid races.
They are oviparous, meaning they lay eggs to bring forth their offspring. The process
involves a complex courtship ritual where potential mates demonstrate their strength,
prowess, and compatibility. Once a pair has formed a bond, the female lays eggs that are
carefully nurtured and protected by both parents until they hatch.
It is important to note that Drakarim genders do not exhibit exterior physical
differences, making it challenging for outsiders to discern the gender of an individual
based solely on appearance. Gender roles and distinctions are primarily determined
through societal norms and cultural expectations.
Complex Kinship
The Drakarim maintain a complex web of relationships with the various races of
Ryndor. Their connections with other races are often influenced by their deep-rooted
reverence for dragons and their shared affinity for Draconic culture.

The Drakarim have a particularly close bond with the Leoporin, as both races
share a deep connection to nature and the wild. They often collaborate in matters of
conservation, hunting, and exploration, appreciating each other's agility and
resourcefulness.
With the Aviari, the Drakarim often find common ground in their shared love for
the skies. Both races have a deep affinity for flight and a profound appreciation for the
freedom it brings. They engage in aerial displays, exchange knowledge about flying
creatures, and occasionally form alliances to protect their territories from common
threats.
The relationship between the Drakarim and the Cervar is characterized by a
mutual respect for strength and honor. Both races value martial prowess and often
engage in friendly competitions and martial training. The Drakarim find the Cervar's
disciplined nature and unwavering loyalty appealing, fostering a bond built on trust and
camaraderie.
The Drakarim's relationship with humans is more complex and strained due to
their storied history with dragons, which often influences human perceptions of the
Drakarim. While some humans view the Drakarim with awe and fascination, others
harbor fear and prejudice, viewing them as dangerous and unpredictable.
The Drakarim, in turn, may approach human interactions with caution, mindful
of the potential for misunderstanding and conflict. However, there are instances of
Drakarim individuals who strive to bridge the gap and foster understanding between
their kind and humans, hoping to heal the wounds of the past.
The Drakarim maintain a respectful but somewhat distant relationship with the
Dwarves and Elves. They appreciate the Dwarves' craftsmanship and resilience,
occasionally seeking their expertise in forging powerful weapons and armor. As for the
Elves, the Drakarim admire their wisdom and affinity for magic, sometimes seeking
their guidance in matters of spirituality and nature. However, due to their distinct
cultures and priorities, the Drakarim may not have extensive interactions with these
races, maintaining a respectful distance while acknowledging their unique strengths.
Mother Mountain
The ancestral lands of the Drakarim, known as Drakemount, are a realm of aweinspiring beauty and rugged grandeur. Nestled within the towering peaks of Mt.
Bannockwyrm, or "Mother Mountain" to the Drakarim, Drakemount encompasses a
vast expanse of diverse landscapes and sacred sites. At the heart of this land lies the
majestic capital city of Dra'Zirath, a breathtaking metropolis nestled in the shadow of
Benard Peak, the tallest peak in all of Ryndor.
Deep within the heart of Drakemount, nestled within the Veil of Embers, lies the
Dragon's Maw, a colossal volcanic caldera spewing forth plumes of ash and fire. This
sacred site is believed to be the birthplace of the first Drakarim, where their connection
to dragonkind was forged. The Eternal Glacier, located in the northern reaches of
Drakemount, is a frozen expanse that stretches as far as the eye can see, its icy beauty a
stark contrast to the fiery realms of the south.
Throughout Drakemount, various smaller settlements dot the landscape, such as

Emberreach, a thriving mining town known for its rich deposits of dragonstone, and
Talonrest, a hidden enclave nestled within a series of soaring cliffside caves. These
settlements serve as important cultural and strategic hubs, fostering the close-knit
community and resilience of the Drakarim people.
Drakemount, with its majestic peaks, fiery landscapes, and hidden wonders, is a
testament to the enduring legacy of the Drakarim. It is a land of mythical splendor,
where the echoes of ancient dragons still reverberate, inspiring the Drakarim to
embrace their heritage and protect the sacred bond they share with their draconic
ancestors.
Brutal Tongue
The language of the Drakarim is a guttural and powerful tongue, resonating with
primal strength and raw emotion. It is a language forged in the crucible of their fiery
ancestry, carrying the echoes of ancient dragons and the weight of their storied history.
Each word is pronounced with a thunderous intensity, as if it carries the weight of a
dragon's roar.
The phonetics of the Drakarim language are characterized by harsh, rasping
sounds and deep, resonant tones. It is a language that demands strength and presence,
reflecting the ferocity and tenacity of the Drakarim people. Their words carry a sense of
authority and power, spoken with an unwavering conviction.
To the untrained ear, the Drakarim language may sound brutal and intimidating,
filled with sharp consonants and rolling syllables. The vocalizations often mimic the
sounds of roaring flames, hissing serpents, and the clash of steel, evoking the primal
forces of nature and the untamed power of dragons.
Drakarim Phrases
"In the eyes of dragons, the scales of truth are never hidden."
This phrase highlights the Drakarim's reverence for dragons and their connection
to truth and wisdom. It suggests that the true nature and intentions of individuals can
be discerned by the discerning gaze of a dragon.
"Words are but embers, deeds are the inferno."
This expression emphasizes the Drakarim's emphasis on action and the
significance they place on deeds over mere words. It reflects their belief that actions
speak louder than empty promises.
"A dragon's tale told thrice becomes eternal lore."
This coloquialism highlights the Drakarim reverence for storytelling and oral
traditions. It suggests that a story of great significance and wisdom gains timeless value
when it is passed down and retold multiple times, ensuring its perpetuity in the annals
of Drakarim history.
Dragonshrines
The religion of the Drakarim is deeply rooted in their reverence for dragons and
their divine essence. They believe that dragons are not only mighty and majestic

creatures but also divine beings embodying aspects of power, wisdom, and primal
forces of nature.
Their religious practices center around the worship and veneration of dragon
deities and the acknowledgment of their influence on the world.
Drakarim religious ceremonies often take place in sacred spaces known as
Dragonshrines, where dragon effigies and relics are displayed. These shrines serve as
places of devotion and contemplation, where Drakarim offer prayers, sacrifices, and
perform rituals to honor the dragon deities. The rituals may involve chanting ancient
hymns, making offerings of precious metals or gemstones, or reenacting mythical
dragon tales through elaborate performances.
The religion of the Drakarim emphasizes the concepts of power, honor, and
ancestral connection. They believe in the divine lineage of dragons, considering
themselves to be descendants or chosen children of these magnificent beings. They
strive to emulate the virtues of dragons, such as strength, wisdom, and self-control,
and seek to achieve spiritual enlightenment and communion with the dragon deities.
While dragon worship forms the core of their religious practices, the Drakarim
also revere the natural world and its elements. They see the world as an interconnected
web of energies and believe in the balance and harmony of nature. Some Drakarim
priests and spiritual leaders, known as Scalebinders, possess the ability to commune
with dragons and interpret their will, acting as intermediaries between the mortal
realm and the divine dragon realm.
The religion of the Drakarim is not strictly organized or unified, with variations
and regional differences in specific beliefs and practices. However, the underlying
reverence for dragons and the pursuit of spiritual enlightenment through their
guidance remain central tenets of their faith.
For Honor and Renown
Driven by honor, glory, a thirst for knowledge, devotion to dragons, or a quest for
justice, Drakarim adventurers seek fame, respect, exploration, and the protection of
their kin. Their passion for proving themselves in battle, uncovering ancient secrets,
and defending dragonkind fuels their desire for adventure and shapes their path in the
world.
Barbarian Drakarim Barbarians tap into their primal instincts and the ferocity of
their draconic bloodline, becoming formidable warriors on the battlefield. They unleash
their rage, gaining increased strength, durability, and the ability to shrug off damage,
embodying the raw power of their ancestors.
Fighter Drakarim Fighters are disciplined warriors, honing their combat skills
and tactics to perfection. With their strong physical attributes and natural affinity for
weaponry, they become versatile fighters capable of wielding a wide range of weapons
and adopting various fighting styles to suit their preferred approach to combat.
Sorcerer Drakarim Sorcerers inherit their innate magical abilities from their
draconic lineage. They can tap into the raw arcane power that flows through their veins,
casting spells that harness the elements, manipulate energy, and evoke the primal
forces of nature. Their magic is a testament to their deep connection with dragons.

\pagebreakNum
Warlock Drakarim Warlocks forge pacts with powerful dragons or other draconic
entities, gaining access to forbidden knowledge and mystical abilities. They make deals
with their patrons, exchanging their loyalty and service for magical powers that grant
them eldritch invocations, otherworldly spells, and the ability to command the forces of
dragons.
Paladin Drakarim Paladins are devoted champions who embody the ideals of
honor, justice, and the mighty dragons they revere. They wield their martial prowess
alongside divine magic, smiting their foes with righteous fury and protecting their allies
